Available regions, deployment templates and instance configurationsedit

Click any row to view the details for that region.

Google Cloud Platformedit

Taiwan (asia-east1), gcp-asia-east1

Available templates

Template ID Name Description

gcp-compute-optimized

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-compute-optimized-v2

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-storage-optimized-v2

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

gcp-storage-optimized

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

gcp-memory-optimized-v2

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-memory-optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-storage-optimized-dense-v2

Storage optimized (dense)

Ideal for ingestion use cases with more than 10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases with very large data sets.

gcp-storage-optimized-dense

Storage optimized (dense)

Ideal for ingestion use cases with more than 10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases with very large data sets.

gcp-general-purpose-v2

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-general-purpose

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

gcp-cpu-optimized-v2

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

gcp-hot-warm

Hot-Warm Architecture

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

gcp-appsearch-dedicated

App Search

Easily implement powerful search experiences for your website, app, or workplace with refined APIs and tools.

gcp-cross-cluster-search

Cross Cluster Search

Search data across one or more associated remote deployments.

gcp-enterprise-search-dedicated

Enterprise Search

Add a search experience to your website, applications, or search the apps you use at work.

gcp-observability

Observability

Use logs, metrics, and APM data to monitor and react to to events in your environment.

gcp-security

Security

Prevent, detect, and respond to threats with SIEM, endpoint security, and threat hunting.

gcp-io-optimized-v2

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

gcp-io-optimized

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

Template ID Name Description

gcp-compute-optimized

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-compute-optimized-v2

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-storage-optimized

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

gcp-memory-optimized-v2

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-memory-optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-storage-optimized-dense

Storage optimized (dense)

Ideal for ingestion use cases with more than 10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases with very large data sets.

gcp-general-purpose

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

gcp-hot-warm

Hot-Warm Architecture

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

gcp-appsearch-dedicated

App Search

Easily implement powerful search experiences for your website, app, or workplace with refined APIs and tools.

gcp-cross-cluster-search

Cross Cluster Search

Search data across one or more associated remote deployments.

gcp-enterprise-search-dedicated

Enterprise Search

Add a search experience to your website, applications, or search the apps you use at work.

gcp-observability

Observability

Use logs, metrics, and APM data to monitor and react to to events in your environment.

gcp-security

Security

Prevent, detect, and respond to threats with SIEM, endpoint security, and threat hunting.

gcp-io-optimized-v2

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

gcp-io-optimized

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

Available templates

Template ID Name Description

gcp-compute-optimized

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-compute-optimized-v2

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-storage-optimized

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

gcp-memory-optimized-v2

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-memory-optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-storage-optimized-dense

Storage optimized (dense)

Ideal for ingestion use cases with more than 10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases with very large data sets.

gcp-general-purpose

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

gcp-hot-warm

Hot-Warm Architecture

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

gcp-appsearch-dedicated

App Search

Easily implement powerful search experiences for your website, app, or workplace with refined APIs and tools.

gcp-cross-cluster-search

Cross Cluster Search

Search data across one or more associated remote deployments.

gcp-enterprise-search-dedicated

Enterprise Search

Add a search experience to your website, applications, or search the apps you use at work.

gcp-observability

Observability

Use logs, metrics, and APM data to monitor and react to to events in your environment.

gcp-security

Security

Prevent, detect, and respond to threats with SIEM, endpoint security, and threat hunting.

gcp-io-optimized-v2

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

gcp-io-optimized

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

Available templates

Template ID Name Description

gcp-compute-optimized

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-compute-optimized-v2

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

gcp-storage-optimized

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

gcp-memory-optimized-v2

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-memory-optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

gcp-storage-optimized-dense

Storage optimized (dense)

Ideal for ingestion use cases with more than 10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases with very large data sets.

gcp-general-purpose

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

gcp-hot-warm

Hot-Warm Architecture

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

gcp-appsearch-dedicated

App Search

Easily implement powerful search experiences for your website, app, or workplace with refined APIs and tools.

gcp-cross-cluster-search

Cross Cluster Search

Search data across one or more associated remote deployments.

gcp-enterprise-search-dedicated

Enterprise Search

Add a search experience to your website, applications, or search the apps you use at work.

gcp-observability

Observability

Use logs, metrics, and APM data to monitor and react to to events in your environment.

gcp-security

Security

Prevent, detect, and respond to threats with SIEM, endpoint security, and threat hunting.

gcp-io-optimized-v2

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

gcp-io-optimized

I/O Optimized

Use for for all-purpose workloads, including time-series data like logs and metrics.

Storage optimized (dense)

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

gcp-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

General purpose

Memory Optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

Storage optimized

azure-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

azure-compute-optimized-v2

Compute Optimized

Designed for search-heavy workloads.

azure-general-purpose

General purpose

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 5-7 days of data available for fast access. Also good for search workloads with less-frequent indexing and medium to high querying loads. Provides a balance of storage, memory, and CPU.

azure-memory-optimized-v2

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

azure-memory-optimized

Memory Optimized

Best for small data sets and low query loads.

azure-storage-optimized

Storage optimized

Good for most ingestion use cases with 7-10 days of data available for fast access. Also good for light search use cases without heavy indexing or CPU needs.

azure-cpu-optimized

CPU optimized

Suitable for ingestion use cases with 1-4 days of data available for fast access and for search use cases with indexing and querying workloads. Provides the most CPU resources per unit of RAM.

azure-hot-warm

Hot-Warm Architecture

Useful for time-series analytics that benefit from automatic index curation.

azure-appsearch-dedicated

App Search

Easily implement powerful search experiences for your website, app, or workplace with refined APIs and tools.

azure-cross-cluster-search

Cross Cluster Search

Search data across one or more associated remote deployments.

azure-enterprise-search-dedicated

Enterprise Search

Add a search experience to your website, applications, or search the apps you use at work.

azure-observability

Observability

Use logs, metrics, and APM data to monitor and react to to events in your environment.

azure-security

Security

Prevent, detect, and respond to threats with SIEM, endpoint security, and threat hunting.

azure-io-optimized-v2

I/O Optimized

Ideal for time-series data, such as logs and metrics.

azure-io-optimized

I/O Optimized

Ideal for time-series data, such as logs and metrics.

azure-io-optimized-v3

I/O Optimized

Ideal for time-series data, such as logs and metrics.
